 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Strength in Microsoft Cloud Highlights Q3 Results </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Increasing usage of Microsoft Azure, Office 365, Bing and Xbox
Live contributes to Q3 growth </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:14pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>REDMOND, Wash. &#151; April&nbsp;23, 2015 &#151;</B> Microsoft Corp. today announced that
revenues for the quarter ended March&nbsp;31, 2015 grew to $21.7 billion. Gross margin, operating income, and diluted earnings per share (&#147;EPS&#148;) for the quarter were $14.6 billion, $6.6 billion, and $0.61 per share, respectively.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">These financial results include $190 million of integration and restructuring expenses, or a $0.01 per share negative impact, related
to Microsoft&#146;s restructuring plan announced in July 2014 and the ongoing integration of the Nokia Devices and Services (&#147;NDS&#148;) business. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">During the quarter, Microsoft returned $7.5 billion to shareholders in the form of share repurchases and dividends. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">The following table notes the impact of the integration and restructuring expenses on the company&#146;s financial performance (&#147;Noted
Items&#148;). This financial information is provided to aid investors in better understanding the company&#146;s performance. All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

quarter. Excluding the effect of foreign exchange rate changes on the GAAP amounts, on a constant currency basis, revenue and gross margin would have grown 9% and 4%, respectively, and operating income and EPS would have declined 4% and 7%,
respectively. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;Customers continue to choose Microsoft to transform their business and as a result we saw incredible growth across
our cloud services this quarter,&#148; said Satya Nadella, chief executive officer at Microsoft. &#147;Next week at Build we&#146;re excited to share more about how we&#146;re empowering every individual and organization on the planet to achieve
more with the next generation of our platforms.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;We executed with strong operational and financial discipline again this
quarter, and are seeing positive impact from our investments in key growth areas,&#148; said Amy Hood, chief financial officer at Microsoft.&nbsp;&#147;We remain focused on maximizing shareholder value and again increased our overall return of
capital to shareholders.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Devices and Consumer revenue grew 8% (up 11% in constant currency) to $9.0 billion, with the following

webcast. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Webcast Details </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT

Relations, will host a conference call and webcast at 2:30 p.m. PDT (5:30 p.m. EDT) today to discuss details of the company&#146;s performance for the quarter and certain forward-looking information. The session may be accessed at </FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#a9f866">http://www.microsoft.com/investor</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#666666">. The webcast will be available for replay through the close of business on April&nbsp;23, 2016. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Constant Currency </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">We
present constant currency information to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect of foreign currency rate fluctuations. To present this information, current and comparative prior period results
for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are converted into United States dollars using the average exchange rates from the comparative period rather than the actual exchange rates in effect during the respective
periods. The non-GAAP financial measures presented below should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period
in the last fiscal year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Financial Performance Constant Currency Reconciliation </B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Integration and restructuring expenses were $190 million during the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2015. Integration and restructuring expenses
include employee severance expenses and costs associated with the consolidation of facilities and manufacturing operations, including asset write-downs and contract termination costs, resulting from Microsoft&#146;s restructuring plan. Integration
and restructuring expenses also include systems consolidation and other business integration expenses, as well as transaction fees and direct acquisition costs, associated with the acquisition of NDS. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>About Microsoft </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Founded
in 1975, Microsoft (Nasdaq &#147;MSFT&#148;) is the worldwide leader in software, services, devices, and solutions that help people and businesses realize their full potential. </FONT></P>
